<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:etymology.html>Etymology</a> 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:lighten.html>lighten</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">lihten</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">līhtan</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">lȳhtan</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">lēohtan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lighten.html>lighten</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:illuminate.html>illuminate</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:give.html>give</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:light.html>light</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:shine.html>shine</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:grow.html>grow</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:light.html>light</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dawn.html>dawn</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:light.html>light</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:kindle.html>kindle</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*liuhtijaną</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*leuhtą</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*-janą</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:cognate.html>Cognate</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">leuchten</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:shine.html>shine</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
